## âš¡ What is Shortcuts?

<div align="center">
<img src="assets/shortcuts-logo.png" width="100" height="auto" />
</div>

Shortcuts is a powerful app built into Apple devices (iPhone, iPad, Mac, etc.) that lets you create custom automations, with One Single Tap.

According to [Appleâ€™s official guide](https://support.apple.com/guide/shortcuts/welcome/ios), â€œA shortcut provides a quick way to get things done with your apps, with just a tap or by asking Siri. The Shortcuts app lets you create your own shortcuts with multiple steps."

Whether you want to _open your favorite playlist_, _schedule Reminders_, _batch-edit photos_, _get directions to the next event on your Calendar_, or even _generate expense reports_â€•Shortcuts makes it possible. All from the device in your _pocket_.

With **Shortcuts**, the potential is pretty much **endless**!

## ğŸ“š Story

I first discovered ï£¿ Apple Shortcuts in November 2022 while trying to streamline a few repetitive tasks on my iPhone.

Over time, I realized how much these simple â€œappletsâ€ were transforming my daily life. What started as a curiosity quickly turned into a game changerâ€”the more I built and used them, the more they help me to _save time_, _reduce friction_, and _reclaim control over how I use my phone_.

It made too big of a difference to keep to myselfâ€”so I decided to make it public and become a Shortcuts evangelist, committed to show people what was possible and how it could make their lives easier, just like it did for me.

## ğŸ›¤ï¸ Mission

> â€œMy central claim in this book is that these two trendsâ€”overprotection in the real world and underprotection in the virtual worldâ€”are the major reasons why children born after 1995 became the anxious generation.â€
â€• Jonathan Haidt, _The Anxious Generation: How the Great Rewiring of Childhood Is Causing an Epidemic of Mental Illness_

We live in a digital age where technology has reshaped nearly every aspect of our daily lives.

While this technological revolution has brought countless benefits, it has also introduced significant challengesâ€”particularly in how it affects focus, well-being, and the development of children and adolescents.

Thatâ€™s where **[Shortcutomation](https://shortcutomation.com)** comes in: **help people take back their time**, by simplifying digital routines using ï£¿ Apple Shortcuts.

We believe a world where your phone *serves* you, not *distracts* you.

A world without cluttered apps.

A world free of mindless doomscrolling.

A world where people click less, scroll less, type less.

A world where everyone lives a calmer, more present and intentional lifeâ€”focused on what truly matters in the real world.

1. Visit the [Gallery](https://shortcutomation.com/gallery) on the website, or browse the shortcut folders above.

2. Choose a category that interests you:
   - **Recommended:** Start with **[Standalone Fun](https://shortcutomation.com/gallery/standalone%20fun)** â€” these shortcuts run immediately without any setup.
   - For other categories, check the **Dependencies** and **Required Apps** sections on each shortcut's page to get everything you need.

3. On each shortcut page, you'll find three buttons:
   - **Preview Shortcut** (in a HTML page)
   - **Download Shortcut** (via an iCloud shared link)
   - **View Source Code** (on GitHub)

4. Add shortcuts to your device

**Contributions are always welcome!**

[![Suggest a Shortcut](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸ’¡_Suggest%20a%20Shortcut-purple?style=for-the-badge)](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/issues/new?labels=enhancement&template=feature-request---.md)
[![Report a Bug](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸ_Report%20a%20Bug-red?style=for-the-badge)](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/issues/new?labels=bug&template=bug-report---.md)
[![Ask a Question](https://img.shields.io/badge/â“_Ask%20a%20Question-yellow?style=for-the-badge)](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/issues/new?labels=question&template=ask-question---.md)

If you have any new shortcut or automation ideas, feel free to [fork the repository](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/fork) and [submit a pull request](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/compare).

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md) for full guidelines and helpful tips to get started.

Alternatively, you can [open an issue](https://github.com/huaminghuangtw/Shortcutomation/issues/new?labels=enhancement&template=feature-request---.md) to suggest a shortcut or automation idea.
